########
By Aaron0000

Modifies a large number of class mods to be more balanced, fitting, specialized, or otherwise interesting.

NOTE;
Due to "brilliance" from Gearbox and the Unreal Engine, modifying the Shot com for Assassins causes the game to take a screenshot every time the mod is activated.
If using Sir Umnei's Allegiance Class Mods patch, load it after this one for it to function properly.

Credit and thanks to Sir Umnei for fixing the UI issues.
########
If a class mod replaces skills, I have given the variant of that class mod a new prefix to match it. Said prefixes are listed at the end of each of the upcoming, respective lines.

Salvador
---------
*Note: Any class mods that boost Inconcievable boost it at reduced rates. You can only reach a maximum of 90% chance to not consume ammo.

Beast - Now boosts Ainâ€™t Got Time to Bleed instead of Just Got Real. Boosts explosive damage instead of health capacity. (Brazen Beast)
Devastator - Now boosts Inconcievable instead of Filled to the Brim. (Perpetual Devastator)
Monk - Now boosts All in the Reflexes instead of Sexual Tyrannosaurus.
Raider - Now boosts movement speed instead of assault rifle accuracy.
Renegade - Now boosts Divergent Likeness instead of All I Need is One. (Pragmatic Renegade)
Titan - Nows boosts Sexual Tyrannosaurus and Ain't Got Time to Bleed instead of Out of Bubblegum and I'm the Juggarnaut. (Altered Titan, Brazen Tian)
War Dog - Now boosts Inconcievable instead of Filled to the Brim. (Perpetual War Dog)


Axton
-----
Rifleman - Now boosts Assault Rifle critical hit damage instead of magazine size.
Tactician - Now boosts Pressure and Quick Charge instead of Battlefront and Resourceful. (Juiced Tactician and Security Tactician)
Veteran - Now boosts Ready instead of Last Ditch Effort. (Warfare Veteran)


Zer0
----
Infiltrator - Now boosts Rising Sh0t and F0ll0wthr0ugh instead of Unf0rseen and Ir0n Hand. (Disturbed Infiltrator and Shadow Infiltrator)
Ninja - Now boosts F0ll0thr0ugh instead of Resurgence. (Swift Ninja)
Professional - Now boosts Grim and Fast Hands instead of Ambush and Tw0 Fang. (Grim Professional and Wily Professional)
Rogue - Now boosts Innervate instead of Like the Wind.
Shot - Now boosts 0ne Sh0t 0ne Kill, Tw0 Fang, and Rising Sh0t instead of 0ptics, Precisi0n, and Kill C0nfirmed. (One Shot, Unequaled Shot, Disturbed Shot)
Sniper - Now boosts Killer instead of Precisi0n. (The Sniper)
Spy - Now boosts Grim instead of Vel0city. (Grim Spy)
Stalker - Now boosts Innervate instead of C0unterstrike. (Excited Stalker)
Survivor - Now boosts Grim and Fearless instead of Ambush and Rising Sh0t. (Grim Survivor and Unpredictable Survivor)
Legendary Sniper - Now boosts Killer instead of Precisi0n. Replaced Shield capacity penalty with slow Sniper Rifle Ammo Regeneration.


Maya
----
Banshee - Now boosts Accelerate and Quicken instead of Immolate and Backdraft. Boosts Fire Rate and Reload Speed instead of Shield Recharge Rate and Shield Delay. Reduces shield capacity instead of health capacity. (Wild Banshee and Consistent Banshee)
Binder - Now boosts Wreck instead of Reaper. (Scheming Binder)
Cleric - Now boosts Foresight instead of Restoration.
Fox - Now boosts Immolate and Backdraft instead of Helios and Blight Phoenix. Boosts Incendiary damage instead of Burn Damage. (Unyielding Fox and Scorched Fox)
Matriarch - Now boosts Reaper instead of Sustenance. (Cunning Matriarch)
Warder - Now boost Inertia instead of Recompense. Boosts Shield Recharge Rate. (Guarded Warder)
Witch - Now boosts Suspension instead of Helios. Boosts Corrosive damage instead of chance and DoT damage. (Chrono Witch)
Legendary Nurse - Now boosts Life Tap instead of Sustenance.


Gaige
-----
Anarchist - Now boosts Unstoppable Force, Typecast Iconoclast, and Phresrunk Cyberpunk instead of Fancy Mathematics, Death from Above, and Annoyed Android. (Punkish Anarchist, Iconic Anarchist, Unstoppable Anarchist)
Catalyst - Now boosts More Pep and Electrical Burn instead of Shock Storm and Wires Don't Talk. (Peppy Catalyst and Scorching Catalyst)
Roboteer - Now boosts 20% Cooler and Annoyed Android instead of Made of Sterner Stuff and Potent as a Pony. (Cool Roboteer and Swift Roboteer)
Technophile - Now boosts Unstoppable Force and Myelin instead of Strength of Five Gorillas and Interspersed Outburst. (Unshockable Technophile and Unstoppable Technophile)
Zapper - Now boosts Shock Storm and Interpersed Outburst instead of Electrical Burn and More Pep. Also actually boosts shock damage (ignore the UI) instead of shock status effect damage now. (Ionized Zapper and Manic Zapper)
Legendary Anarchist - Now boosts Phresrunk Cyberpunk instead of Myelin.
Legendary Catalyst - Now boosts Shock Storm instead of Electrical Burn. Also boosts Shock Damage.


Krieg
-----
Barbarian - Now boosts Blood-Filled Guns and Embrace the Pain instead of Blood Trance and Salt the Wound. 
Crunch - Now boosts Embrace the Pain and Blood-Filled Guns instead of Taste of Blood and Blood Trance. (Pain Crunch and Full Crunch)
Meat - Now boosts Pain is Power instead of Empty the Rage. Boosts Shotgun damage instead of health regeneration. (Power Meat)
Reaper - Now boosts Fire Fiend instead of Fuel the Fire. (Burnt Reaper)
Slab - Now boosts Taste of Blood instead of Fuel the Rampage. Also adds health regeneration. (Dazed Slab)
Torch - Now boosts burn damage resistance along with Burn Damage.
Wound - Now boosts Embrace the Pain and Elemental Elation instead of Taste of Blood and Boiling Blood. (Pain Wound and Razed Wound)
Legendary Reaper - Now boosts Strip the Flesh, Salt the Wound, Embrace the Pain, and Blood-Filled Guns instead of Taste of Blood, Blood Overdrive, Thrill of the Kill, and Fuel the Fire.
Legendary Sickle - Now boosts Salt the Wound instead of Pain is Power.
Legendary Torch - Now boosts Fire Fiend instead of Flame Flare. Also adds burn damage resistance.





---------
RATIONALE

Beast - Just Got Real just kinda sucks, so I gave it a marginally more useful skill. Explosive damage is because 1. more useful than health capacity on a Gunzerker and 2. Torgue.
Devastator -Inconcievable is awesome, and I wanted to open up some more options for useful Gunzerker COMs.
Monk - Monk's already great, but Sexy T-Rex is never used. So I gave it a tier 1 skill that is used often.
Raider - Assault rifle accuracy? Really? Decided to make this one the Money Shot mobbing-counterpart to the Monk's raw damage. Go very fast with Incite and the inherent movement speed buff.
Renegade - Rather than boost a skill that is use once in a blue moon, it'd be better to boost something that makes sense for duel-wielding pistols. Hence Divergent Likeness.
Titan - Wanted to make it more distinct from the Tank. Titan now heavily focuses on health and regeneration, while tank focuses on resisting things and boosting shield.
War Dog - Same reasons as Devastator. Also, I wanted to see what Sal's like with +10/11 5 Shots or 6 and Inconcievable.


Axton
-----
Rifleman - Axton isn't hurting for Assault Rifle magazine size buffs, so I gave the Rifleman COM something more palpable.
Tactician - It already boosted Team Shield Recharge Rate and Team Shield Recharge Delay, so I figured it may as well go full Shield-COM. Should be quite the shield tank.
Veteran - Rather than having a situational skill like Last Ditch Effort, Ready is always active. Also, Tediore-chuckers will appreciate this.


Zer0
----
Infiltrator - It's trying to be a Gun/Melee Hybrid COM, and thus I gave it more useful skills for said purpose.
Ninja - Resurgence is largely invalidated by Moxxi-weapon melee or the Law/Order combo. Gave it something more useful.
Professional - The stat boosts for it are Shield Capacity and Reload speed, so I gave it skills to accentuate that.
Rogue - Like the Wind is (before 3.0 patch) not very useful, as well as placed rather deep into the Bloodshed tree. I replaced it with a skill that is more likely to be picked up by any Zer0 player, not just Melee builds.
Shot - Might as well give the niche Infinity build a bone. Also because two out of three skills had Shot in the title.
Sniper - Killer's simply more useful than Precisi0n in most scenarios.
Spy - To further boost the cooldown rate, as well as indirectly boost Ambush and Unf0rseen.
Stalker - C0unterstrike has nothing to do with pistols. F0ll0thr0ugh, however, has much more use with pistols.
Survivor - Fearless is for when shields are down, and Grim is to help shields get back up. Gives a little punch without having to rely on Rising Sh0t (which is now more prominent in the Shot COM). Glass Tank builds may appreciate this.
Legendary Sniper - Applied normal Sniper COM change. The slow Sniper Rifle Ammo regeneration is there to lend a hand between fights.

Maya
----
Banshee - Banshee's largely only used for Fleet shenanigans, so I decided to make it more speed themed and moved the flamey bits to the Fox COM, hence fire rate and reload buffs. The shield capacity reduction will allow Maya to pull off Sal's/Zer0's Fabled Tortoise trick with lower level Tortoises (because GOTTAGOFAST).
Binder - Wreck is more fitting of a Phaselock-themed Class mod.
Cleric - Restoration is largely unnecessary to invest more than one point into. Foresight is a reasonably more useful skill to invest into.
Fox - Firefox needed some firepower, so now Immolate and Backdraft are there. Incendiary damage boost is there to further up the firepower.
Matriarch - Was treading on Nurse territory, so I gave it Reaper for it to function as a more offensively-inclined health com.
Warder - Between Shield Capacity and Ward, it was trying to be a Shield-focused COM. Inertia serves to accentuate that further, in a manner more useful than Recompense.
Witch - Leave fire to the Fox COM, this ones a bit more Corrosive focused. Suspension is more useful and fits in with the theme of witchcraft (and is more useful than Blight Phoenix would be).
Legendary Nurse - Legendary Nurse isn't running short of ways to regenerate health passively. This gives it a more useful option.


Gaige
-----
Anarchist - Fancy Mathematics and Annoyed Android did not really have a lot to do with the theme of Anarchy. And Death from Above is mediocre.
Catalyst - Zapper and Catalyst were vying for the same role. Catalyst is now more focused on causing DoTs and strengthening them.
Roboteer - Traded bulk for more speed, as well as more frequent use of Deathtrap.
Technophile - It seemed to be trying to be a shield com before. Strength of Five Gorillas and Interspursed Outburst didn't really have much to do with shields. Unstoppable Force and Myelin have quite a lot to do with shields.
Zapper - As mentioned before, Zapper and Catalyst were competing for the same role. Zapper is now the more direct option for electric-themed builds.
Legendary Anarchist - Because it makes sense for the LEGENDARY ANARCHIST to boost how many stacks you can have.
Legendary Catalyst - It now acts as a fusion between the Zapper and Catalyst mods. Should also give Little Big Trouble-builds more viability to compete with the other trees.


Krieg
-----
Barbarian - Before, it seemed like it was trying to do a little bit of everything. Now, with Blood-Filled Guns boosting magazine size, Embrace the Pain boosting fire rate, and Fire Fiend boosting accuracy and reload speed, combined with the stat possibilities of the Tina COMs, it is now a more versatile (and useful) COM.
Crunch - Other than Strip the Flesh, the other skills weren't really contributing to an Explosive-build much. Now it has more useful skills to work with (and Tediore-builds will appreciate the Blood-Filled Guns boost).
Meat - Meat and Slab were competing with each other for the role of health COM. So I turned the Meat COM into a Shotgun-themed COM. Krieg needed a good shotgun COM.
Reaper - Mania/Hellborn builds will be able to relaibly set things on fire during a Buzz Axe Rampage, as well as use Blood Overdrive effectively when not Rampaging.
Slab - Meat and Slab were competing with each other for the role of health COM. So I made the Slab the definitive health COM. Fuel the Rampage is largely useless after getting Release the Beast, so I replaced it with a more useful skill for early game.
Torch - Torch seemed to focus on applying, maintaining, and empowering DoTs before. Now it is a longer-lasting Torch due to the reduced burn damage on the user when equipped.
Wound - Skills are no longer all over the place, now they are focused on putting out as many bullets as possible within a short time.
Legendary Reaper - Most of the time, the Legendary Reaper was used for +10 Blood Bath and extended kill skill duration time. So now the skills have been altered to mesh with that better.
Legendary Sickle - Salt the Wound and Pain is Power apply similar benefits, but Salt the Wound is both far more potent and not reliant on Hellborn.
Legendary Torch - Legendary Torch does not have much difficulty creating and maintaining flames, so it has been replaced with a more useful skill while still leaving the Toast COM as an option for more raw power. Also added the normal Torch COM burn resistance.
